 jisamen likhaa he ki beemaa kaa premium dene ke baad bhi 3000 kisaanon ko clem nahin mila
 Today, farmers reached the Consumer Court in Sirsa, Haryana
 kyonki kareeb 2000 kisaanon kaa beemaa company ne premium lautaa diya taaki clem kii raashi nahin deni pade
 The All India Swaminathan Sangharsh Samiti's Option Pachar spoke about how it could be that the insurance company only returns the premium amount after ten months of taking the premium amount in July 2017, so we have gone to the consumer court
 yahi nahin sirsa zile main 2017 main 68000 kisaanon ne kapaas kaa beemaa karaayaa
 The farmers gave a premium of Rs 500 per acre and the government gave 1500
 to premium kii raashi ho jaati he 2000 prati acre

 kul milakar yah raashi 310 karod kii hoti he

 tab jaakar unhen yah raashi mili he
 Around 320 crore was taken by the farmers, but on their own
 iske baad bhi abhi 2000 kisaanon ko clem kii raashi nahin mili he kyonki beemaa company ne unka premium lautaa diya he
 Farmers have to agitate, go to court, jam the road and then get insurance
 abhi 25 november ko bhaskar main khabar chhapi he ki madhya pradesh ke ashokanagar zile main 70 kisaanon ko beemaa kaa clem milegaa wo bhi 2016 kaa, or wo bhi upabhokta adaalat ke aadesh par
 Farmers filed more letters than agriculture, made rounds of offices, and there was an order to go and meet, they have not been received yet
 yahi nahin pichley saal jo beemaa company hoti he wo is saal badal jaati he
 It is also found that the insurance companies do not have a representative in the district
 kisaan kisase baat kare, kahaan jaae

 hamaare saath aaj pi sainath hai

 200 kisaanon ke sanghathan ko milakar aal india kisaan sangharsh cardination kamity bani he vahi is march kaa aayojan kar rahi he
 Narsinghpur is a village in Atru tehsil of Baran district of Hadauti in Kota district
 is gaanv ke kai kisaanon kii urad or soyabean kii fasal nasht ho gai thi
 For six months, the farmers were making rounds to get insurance
 kabhi beemaa company jate to kabhi bank to kabhi krishi vibhaag
 Bhagirath Sharma said that the Agriculture Department sent three letters to the insurance company that 100% of the crop of these farmers was destroyed
 sari khabaren akhabaaron main chap rahi hai lekin iske baad bhi beemaa kaa paisa nahin mila
 Not only this, the farmers told that the premium amount that banks have deducted has not been passed on to the entire insurance company
 2000 kaa premium katane ke baad beemaa company ke paas 300 rupee pahunche to iskaa matlab he koi bada ghotaalaa he
 Not only this, the amount of insurance was taken from the farmers credit card of all the farmers, but the insurance company returned it saying that not all the crops have been insured
 bhagirath sharma ke kisaan credit card se 4
 a premium amount of Rs 2301 was deducted for 51 acres of crop
 lekin jab soyabean or urad kii fasal nasht hone par beemaa company se sampark kiya gaya to bataaya gaya ki bhagirath sharma kii 4
 51 acres of land is not insured
 maatr 0
 Only 4 acres of land is insured
 216 rupee hi premium mila he, 2301 nahin
 The farmers went to court and the court ordered to sue the insurance company but till date nothing happened
 kisaanon ko beemaa kii raashi nahin mili
 Bhagirath Sharma told one more thing that the farmer has sown the crop of soybean but the bank has written Urad, cutting the insurance premium
 yah bhi hua he taaki kisaan inhen sabamein uljhe rah jaaen or beemaa company ko paise na dene paden
 Bhagirath ji told that the insurance company which was in the district last year is not this year
 uski jagah nai company aa gai he

 nepal main 81 saal baad itnaa bhayanakbukamp aayaa he
 The real cause of earthquake is the rapid movement in the tectonical plates, not only the meteor impact and also due to volcanic eruptions, mine testing and nuclear testing
 jaaniye bukamp se jude 10 tathy:1
 The earth is made up of four layers - inner core, outer core, mantle and crust
 crust or upree mental ko lithosphere kaha jaataa he
 Lithosphere is 50 km thick layer
 ye parat virgon main banty he or inhen tectonical plates kehete hai
 Earthquakes occur when the movement in these tectonical plates intensifies
 yahi nahin ulka ke prabhaav or jwalamukhi visphot or mine testing or newclear testing kii vajah sebhi bukamp atehain
 2
 ab tak kaa sabase bada record kiya gaya bukamp 22 may1960 ko chile main aayaa tha
 This 9
 5 megnitude tivrata kaa bukamp tha
 3
 chile ke baad ab tak kaa sabase bada bukamp 28 march 1964 main united stats main record kiya gaya tha
 This 9
 2 megnitude kaa tha, isse prince wiliam sound, alaska kaa kshetra kaaphi prabhavit hua tha
 4
 kya aapako maaloom he ki bukamp se pehle naharon, naalon or talabon main se ajeeb si khushboo aane lagati he
 This happens because the gases under the earth start coming out
 yahi nahin ground water kaa taapmaana bhibukamp se pehlebadhane lagata he
 5
 alaska sabase zyada bukamp vaala rajya or duniya kaa sabase sismikali active kshetra he
 About 7 in this area
 0 magnidude ke bukamp har saal aate hai
 Not only this, it is common for earthquakes of about 8 magnitudes and above to occur once in 14 years
 6
 There are millions of earthquakes every year
 lekin inaki tivrata kam hoti he
 You might not know that the National Earthquake Information Center records about 20,000 earthquakes every year, of which 100 are earthquakes that cause damage
 7
 You might not know that an earthquake lasts for a few seconds or a few minutes
 lekin ab tak ke itihaas main sabase zyada der tak rahane vaala bukamp 2004 main hind mahaasaagar main aayaa tha
 The earthquake lasted for 10 minutes
 8
 The Shanxi China earthquake of 1556 was the most terrible earthquake ever, killing 830,000 people
 9
 The energy generated by the earthquake is 100 times more than the energy released from the atomic bomb in Japan in 1945
 10
 The Richter scale measuring earthquake intensity was developed by American scientist Charles Richter in 1935
 richter scale par prayek agali ikai pichhali ikai kii tulana main 10 guna adhik tivrata rakhti he
 2 on this scale
 0 yaa 3
 An earthquake of magnitude 0 is mild, while 6
 2 kii tivrata kaa matlab shaktishaalee bukamp hota he

 yah film isi shuukravaar 17 june ko relies honi he
 The counsel for the filmmakers who filed the case in the Bombay High Court said, "the court has rejected the cbfc's review committee's demand for 13 cuts and passed the film with one cut
" jis seen ko film se nikaala gaya he, usamen hero saarvajanik rup se peshaab karata dikhaaya gaya he, jise film se nikaalane ke liye ham pehle hi taiyaar ho gaye the
 ' isse pehle, hoicourt ne kaha tha ki use film "udata punjab" main kahin bhi bhartiya samprabhutaa yaa akhandta par sawaal uthta nahin dikhaai diya
 The High Court said, "we read the entire script to know whether the film promotes intoxication or not
 hamane ye paaya ki film kisi shahar yaa rajya ke naam, yaa phir kisi sanket ke madhyam se bhartiya samprabhutaa yaa akhandta par sawaal uthaati nahin dikhaai detii he
 "saying this, the court said that unless creative freedom is misused, no one should interfere
 tippaniyan The court said that we did not see anything in the film that portrayed a false image of Punjab or affected India's sovereignty or integrity as claimed by the CBFC
 court ne is film se jude vivaad par kaha, sibiefasi ko kanoon ke hisaab se filmon ko sensor karne kaa adhikaar nahin he kyonki sensor shabd cinematograph adhinium main shaamil nahin kiya gaya he
 By the way, there may be some cuts in 'udta Punjab'
 film main istemaal gaaliyon ke paksh main di gai daleelon se bambe hoicourt sahamat nahin he
 It is worth mentioning that on Friday itself, the High Court had reminded the censor board chief Pahlaj Nihalani that his job is to give certificates to the films and not to cut them
 nihlani ne anuraag kashyap kii film "udata punjab" ko praaanpatr dene se pehle film ke 89 drishyon par kanchi chalaa di thi, jiske baad kashyap or unki phantum filmas maamle ko court le gaye the
 "udta Punjab" is going to be released on 17 June
 is maamle kii sunwaayee karte hue justise essi dharmadhikari or justise shalini pansaalkar-joshi kii khandpeeth ne sensor board ko film ke liye 'e' pramaan-patr jari karne kaa bhi aadesh diya he
 The film is to be released on this Friday, 17 June
 bombai hoicourt main mukadmaa darj karaane vaale film nirmaataaon ke vakil ne kaha, 'adaalat ne sibiefasi kii punarikshan samiti kii 13 cat kii maang ko khaarij kar diya he or ek cat ke saath film ko paas kar diya he
 In the scene which has been taken out of the film, the hero is shown publicly urinating, which we had already agreed to remove from the film
 ' Earlier, the High Court had said that it did not appear to question Indian sovereignty or integrity anywhere in the film "udta Punjab"
 hoicourt ne kaha, "hamane puri script ye jaanane ke liye padhi ki kya film nashe ko badhaava detii he yaa nahin
 We found that the film does not appear to question Indian sovereignty or integrity through the name of a city or state, or by any indication
 " yah kehete hue court ne kaha ki jab tak ki rachanaatmak swatantraaa kaa durupyog na ho, kisi ko dakhal nahin dena chahie
 The comments court ne kaha ki hamen film main aisa kuch nahin najar aayaa jo punjab kii galat chhavi pesh karata ho yaa bharat kii samprabhutaa yaa akhandta ko prabhavit karata ho jaisaa ki sibiefasi ne daawa kiya he
 The court said on the controversy related to this film, CBFC does not have the right to censor films according to the law as the word censor is not included in the Cinematograph Act
 vaise 'udata punjab' main kuch cat lag sakate hai
 The Bombay High Court does not agree with the arguments made in favor of the abuses used in the film
 gauratlab he ki shuukravaar ko hi hoicourt ne sensor board ke pramukh pehlaaj nihlani ko yaad dilaayaa tha ki unka kaam filmon ko praaanpatr dena he na ki unamem kaat-chhaant karnaa
 Nihalani had scissored 89 scenes of the film before giving the certificate to Anurag Kashyap's "udta Punjab", after which Kashyap and his Phantom Films took the case to court
 "udata punjab" aagaamee 17 june ko pradarshit hone ja rahi he
